1)
The Center of Victory
As winter comes, it feels quite dark even at six o'clock, so it feels early, but the time is the same. 
Regardless of race, culture, or religion, we must unite centered on God. 
The biggest issue in our faith life, especially for religious people, is how to align ourselves with the will of God or the master of our faith. 
This is always a problem.
When we talk about 'religion', there are various religions. Looking at it now, there are Buddhism, Confucianism, Islam, Christianity, and various ethnic-centered religions, among others. Each of these religions has different masters and different paths, but ultimately, they must converge before one God. We can conclude this. After gathering around one center, east, west, north, and south, they must ultimately become one. Who should be the center? They must become one centered on God.
At the time of becoming one, it does not matter what religion one has come through, nor does it matter what ethnicity or historical background one has. The issue is that they must all unite centered on God. 
The problem is unity. It is not that unity is easy; rather, the difficulties in achieving unity are the real issues.
Now, if we consider the end of the world, when God's will can be fulfilled, we must look at what the difficult elements to unite are. The issue of race, that is, the problem of racial diversity, becomes a significant issue. Ultimately, the black and white issue, or the color issue, or the racial issue is a very big problem.
Then, what must be done for religion to unite centered on God? The first thing that must be done is to quickly establish a religious perspective that transcends racial issues in order to resolve such problems. If everyone gathers before God, but then cannot align themselves in unity around racial issues, that religion will be a backward religion.
So, which religion can play a central role in uniting before God? We can conclude that a religion that takes a transcultural and transracial standard as its tradition will take a leading position in uniting centered on God.
From this perspective, Christianity has become a global religion, with many ethnicities entering Christianity, but despite this, it must fulfill its historical mission of uniting, yet it has not done so, and today the issues of black and white and racial issues are still present. This is a matter that God does not favor at all.
Next, what becomes an issue? Culture becomes an issue. The cultures that each ethnicity or nation has gone through will become problematic. Depending on the cultural background, the living environment changes. If we center on God, we must establish a unified way of life centered on God, but the historical complexities of all the different cultures leave complicated issues unresolved.
Now, we can broadly divide cultures into Western and Eastern cultures. While there have been many cultural spheres until now, that is not the issue; if we look at it broadly, we can categorize them into these two. Furthermore, the currently problematic communist culture has emerged as well.
In this light, in order for these to unite centered on one God in the final days, we must achieve cultural unity based on a transcultural standard that transcends East and West. Therefore, the cultural background becomes an issue. The question of whether the East is better or the West is better arises.
Next, what becomes an issue? Then, religion becomes an issue. They always try to hold on to the faith they have believed in centered on their masters. They have always been taught that "we must become one with God through this." Since that has become a tradition, it inevitably becomes a problem. 
Then, issues like private property, money, and knowledge become trivial matters. 
To unite with God, we must abandon what we have valued until now.
Now, what does this mean? Ultimately, whether it is an organization, a nation, or an individual, the problems that people have valued the most throughout history will become significant issues when it comes to uniting centered on God at the end of days. All the issues that were once important will be at stake.
If one loved their parents, they would think, "Oh, I must go with my mother and father." Then they would think, "Ah, I must go with my beloved spouse. I must take my tribe and relatives with me." This kind of mindset becomes problematic. Can that be reconciled?
Therefore, the most valued issues, in other words, the issues that humans have prioritized throughout history, will become significant problems when it comes to uniting with my path. Do you understand? "Yes." The time will come when it will be the biggest problem.
Now, because God knows this in advance, He cannot help but think about how to resolve this issue. The way to resolve it smoothly can be found in how to create an end-time era that can disregard everything.
Now, if you valued the nation, what is the nation? If you valued culture, what is culture? If you valued your parents, what are parents? If you valued your spouse, what is a spouse? If you centered on the family, what is the family? When such a world comes where all these things can be cast aside, it can also become a cause that can automatically resolve such issues.
If all can be cast aside and can unite in the name of God, then from that point on, it can be a new starting point for resolving problems. Does that make sense? "Yes." Therefore, at the end of days, before humans meet and clash, we can deduce that God will carry out such a strategy. So, what do you think? When the Lord comes, will it be easy for everyone to embrace and come together to become one before God, or will it be easier to disregard everything and come together again? Which seems easier? "The latter." (Laughter) Is that so?
Then what happens? In disregarding everything, eventually, they will disregard even God and Satan. There will be no gods or anything. This is how it will be. (Laughter) When that time comes, it will be both a time of great darkness and a time of great hope. We can understand this here.
For example, such a time will come because this time is approaching. (While writing on the board, he speaks) Therefore, at any time, the intersection point will inevitably lead to the disappearance of two currents, resulting in a chaotic dark age, and a new beginning will emerge. This is the time of intersection.
Until now, humanity has lived within the realm of the fall. We live within the realm of the fall. Now, is this America the nation of God? What kind of nation is this? "The nation of God." Huh? What kind of nation is this? Think about it. Can it be called the nation of God? "No." Then is it the nation of Satan? "No." You don't know, do you? (Laughter) Whose nation is it? Ultimately, whose nation is it? It is the nation of America. That is the only conclusion. When we ask what kind of America it is, we do not know if it is Satan's America or God's America. Who is it? Is it President Ford? Is it you? Are you the owners of this nation?
An eternal and absolute being must be the owner of this land.
I mentioned this briefly yesterday. When we think about this land, the land is eternal, it goes on forever. But how long does a human live? How long does a human live? Humans live less than a hundred years. How can beings that cannot even live a hundred years claim to govern the land that lasts forever? Does that make sense?
If the land could speak, it would say, "Hey, you little brat, what are you doing here?" That is what the land would say. (Laughter) If you were to ask the land, "Hey, land, how old are you?" it would know its age. The land knows how long it has existed. "Then, when it comes to choosing a master, would you prefer someone older than you or someone younger?" It would undoubtedly prefer an older master. That is the conclusion.
However, if we want to make an eternal being our master, but we claim that someone who cannot even live a hundred years is the master, then that person is a thief. If we think that way, the people of America are thieves before the land. Would the land want to be governed by such people who cannot even live a hundred years? Would the land want to be ruled by such individuals? If there is an eternal and absolute being, and if you ask the land, "Hey, who do you want to make your master?" it would say, "Of course, I want to make the eternal and absolute being my master." Wouldn't that be so? "Yes."
Then what is a person? What is a person? Where did this person come from? Where did it come from? "From God." Have you seen it come from God? "No." Then how do you know? (Laughter) That is the problem. As thinking humans, we cannot just blindly say, "Let's believe in God." How did this happen?
This is a bit of a tangent from what I was trying to say, but since it came up, let me say this before moving on.
Humans created as the central mediators between heaven and earth
Now, when we consider where humans were born, they were not born only from the earth. They were not born only from the earth. Our physical bodies came from the earth. Isn't that right? "Yes." However, the mind cannot come from the earth. Where does the mind originate? That becomes a problem. Although we do not know, there must be some source that can be the master of the mind. Without that, it cannot emerge. It is a result, and the mind cannot be seen as having no source. The existence of that source is very common sense and logical.
Our physical bodies are the result of the earth, but similarly, for the mind to emerge, there must be some causal subject that allows the resultant object to be established. This is theoretical.
When we look at it this way, considering the mind and body, there is a dual structure. Therefore, the life centered on our physical bodies and the life of the mind represent two worlds, and if we separate them, two worlds can begin here. This is why we can find the logic that the materialistic age and the spiritual age will inevitably come in the historical end times.
Ultimately, the world problem is... Today, whether it is democracy, communism, materialism, or idealism, it is all about this. It is a global form that expands from one person, and ultimately, it is a philosophical game trying to represent and solve the problem of one person in the democratic world and the communist world. One looks at the spiritual side, while the other looks at the external side.
So, which of these two people is the center? You say the mind is the subject and the body is the object. Then, if it is a subject-object relationship, why do they fight? Why do they fight? That is the problem. Humans were born representing the earth and were also born representing the spiritual realm; if they were born with a dual structure, why can’t they become one and why do they fight? That is the problem.
Then, what becomes an issue here... So, what is the problem? The problem is, why were humans born this way? If the earth wishes to expel humans who can only live for a hundred years, if it dislikes them, then why were they born? Why were they born? If there is a God, if there is a conscientious center, if there is some absolute being that is central, then why did that absolute being create humans? God created humans from matter, from the earth. The Bible says, "He formed man from the dust of the ground and breathed into his nostrils the breath of life."
Now, we can understand that there must be a common goal agreed upon by God and the earth. What common goal could God and the earth have agreed upon?
Can a spiritual being like God relate to the earth? In order for the spiritual being God to establish a relationship with the earth, there must be a mediating entity that connects them. This conclusion arises that a mediator is necessary to unite them. Isn't that so? Who is that mediator? What is it? It is something that both God needs and the earth needs. If that central being, the mediator, is a person, then that person is quite valuable.
Therefore, no matter how great God is, He cannot establish a relationship with the earth without that mediator. It is the same for the earth. The earth cannot go before God without a person. Thus, that intermediary... If there is a mediator between heaven and earth, what is it for? What is the purpose of needing a mediator? Just like the conflict between the mind and body, it was created to resolve that conflict. It is not a mediator. The mind and body are currently in conflict. You see, the mind and body are fighting.
"Yes." Do you fight? "Yes." Although you are one person, are you walking two paths? "Yes."
So, then, why did what God created become two? That leads to the conclusion that God Himself is a God who is inconsistent. Now, from this perspective, what is wrong here? It is wrong. Do you want to fight like this? "No." Would God want that? "No." Would the earth want that? "No." Everyone doesn't want this, but seeing that this unwanted result has occurred, we can find the conclusion that something is wrong here.
Even setting the Bible aside, from this perspective, it shows that humans have done something wrong. It is wrong. Religion has concluded in one word that it is fallen without pursuing or inferring such things. It is broken, broken. Therefore, it must be fixed. To fix it, there must be a blueprint from before it broke. Do you understand? The original blueprint... that is the problem.
So, what we need to think about here is, why did God create humans, and why did the earth cooperate with God to create humans? What is the central goal and focal point? It is not to represent the individual called me.
Only absolute love can make one with God.
When we consider the question of why God created humans, was it because He wanted to? No. Was it to see? No. Why did He create them? He created them to seek love. You need to understand that.
In today's established churches, they think that because God is love, He can love even alone. They believe that even alone, love is needed. 
Do you women have love? Do you have love, or not? "......."
Now, men, do you have love? (Laughter) If a woman has love all by herself and keeps saying, "I have love, I have love, my love, my love," it doesn't exist.
Love cannot manifest without a relationship of reciprocity. It cannot be established. That is the principle. The power of love can only operate in the subject-object relationship. Where the subject-object relationship does not exist, love cannot manifest. Even if it exists, it cannot be shown. Is that right? "Yes." But the creature called man, if he holds a small picture of a woman and likes it, that is normal. But if he does that without anything (expressing with actions), he is crazy, crazy. He has lost his mind. (Laughter)
Now, when we look at it this way, what about God? No matter how absolute God is, if He says, "Oh, my love, my love, my love," alone, that is madness. Even God cannot do that. If there is no object of love, He must find one. Then why did He create humans? The idea that God created humans to seek love is something religion has never even dreamed of until now. Therefore, it concludes that for the absolute God to seek love, humans are absolutely necessary.
What is a person? Are they the subject or the object? "They are the object." Therefore, because humans are the object of the absolute God, they are absolutely necessary. It means they are absolutely needed. This leads to the idea that "Ah, even God has no choice. I am needed. If I am not here... to find that love, they must come to me." Doesn't that feel good? (Laughter)
Next, what about God, and why did the earth cooperate with God to create humans? What is the joint resolution between the earth and God? It is that both need love, so let’s create someone who can make both happy. The earth said, "Let’s do that," and God said, "Let’s do that," and they created humans. We can find that there must be a subject of joint resolution, and what should that be? There is nothing else. 
The conclusion is that there is nothing but love.
To fulfill the theme of love, which is the common goal of God and the earth, they cooperated to create humans. This is a valid conclusion, an ideal conclusion. God is good, the earth is good, and what about humans? Humans are also good. We can conclude that to accomplish this common ideal purpose, God, the earth, and humans are mobilized around humans to pursue that decisive result.
Therefore, what can only create one? What can create one is the absolute love that originally God and the earth wanted and that humans desired the most. This conclusion has no objections, right? "Yes."
The purpose of human birth is to realize God's true love and to fulfill this cosmic love. Humans were born to bear love. The conclusion is that they were born to fulfill God's love and the love of the earth as subjects. Have you thought about such things?
"Oh, I live for knowledge. So I must go to university!" You might think, but do you need knowledge? Do you need knowledge, or do you need love? "Love." Then, do you need money? Do you like gold? Is that what you need, or do you need love? "Love." Do you need power, or do you need love? "Love." Then, do you need life, or do you need love? "Love." You guys, are you saying you would die for love? Can you die? You must live, right? "I can die." When did you think that? (Laughter) Then, is it useful? Is it useful then? (Laughter) Seeing that, we have come very close to what God desires, what the earth desires, and what humanity desires. So that is useful.
When we see such things, would God say, "Why are you like this?" Would God be happy? Would the earth be happy or sad? Everyone is happy, all. What is the purpose of humans being born and living? They live to complete cosmic love, a fact they never even dreamed of.
Therefore, by my completion, I can liberate God from seeking love, and by my completion, I can liberate the earth from seeking subjective love, the love of a master. Then humanity itself can be happy because it has completed everything, having finished all tasks.
Look. The question of who the completion of cosmic love depends on... Of course, it depends on God, but it also depends on humans. Now, when this is the case, the logic that Jesus said one life is greater than the universe is all clarified. Now, doesn't that make humans feel proud? "It makes us feel proud." Therefore, in establishing this love, we can acquire the rights of humans and the rights of the universe.
So, have you tasted God's love? "Yes." Yes? How is it? Is it tasty, or how is it? (Laughter) What is the taste of God's love? It is the most comprehensive taste of everything. That is how it is. (Laughter) That means that if you hold it because you like it, you can hold it endlessly, and if you spread it, you can spread it endlessly.
Therefore, centered on love, you can fill anywhere, and centered on love, you can reach anywhere. Do you understand that? "Yes." Do people in love hug each other, or hold hands and say, "Oh, I love you"? How do they do it? Probably like that. Their eyes pop out, and they want to hug until their noses and mouths are running. I believe that will happen. (Laughter) Do you think so? "Yes." Those uncles will all know. They know because they have loved, all of them. That's right. And they don’t just stand still while hugging. They spin around. From there... that is how the universe revolves in love. Do you understand that? Right? Do you think so? "Yes."
Therefore, what is the taste of love... Therefore, once you get drunk on that love, all your nerves cannot help but become one. There is nowhere else to go. There is nowhere to go. The cells of the eyes, the cells of the nose, the cells of the ears, and all the cells of the body are concentrated there. Do you understand that? It should be that way, right? "Yes."
So, the absolute God loves with a strength that is as strong as that of holding tightly just because He likes it. If the absolute God loves, does He say, "Oh, I am the absolute God, so let’s do this much"? The absolute God also opens His eyes... (expressing with actions) that is how He thinks. Think about how strong that would be. (Laughter) But no matter how absolute God is, He cannot freely manipulate the power of love. Above all, love is the strongest. That is the case. Therefore, when God loves "true love," all of God's nerves and strength concentrate there. God is also absent-minded there.
You know, in first love... even among the fallen humans of today, when they love, they say, "Oh, I could die or live." What would happen if God tasted that love? He would say that even if He dies, He only needs that love. God is the same.
If God found a partner to love like that, would He dance or be sad? He would dance. He would dance and sing and make a fuss.
Then, if God sings and reveals Himself, the whole universe will resonate, and if God does that, America will boom, Korea will boom, and the earth will shake. Do you think that would happen, or not? Do you think so? "Yes." 
Now, if this earth has been born, if it has a birthday, what is the joyful day? It is the day of love, and it is the wish of the earth to feel joy and laughter when God's fingertips touch and His toes touch. Don’t you want that? "We want that." 
These days, people like to go to banquets invited by the president, but is that the problem? Do you want to attend one? "Yes." You already have the invitation. The invitation was given long before the historical era. It has all been given. Do you know you received the invitation? You guys, you don’t even know that. You didn’t know, but know that you have received an invitation. Anyone can go.
Now from this time on, know that God has already sent me an invitation to attend the banquet, and I have it. Do you understand? It is certain. So, does that feel good? "Yes." You have many desires. (Laughter) That is the case. In fact, that is the case.
So why was a person born? To realize God's true love and to fulfill this cosmic love, humans were born, which today no religious person, philosopher, or anyone else has thought about. Did you know that? Did you know? Now do you know? "Yes." So now, by realizing God's love... that is the happiest word.
True love is realized by completely giving oneself.
Here, you young men and women. Some may feel disappointed for not participating in this joint wedding. "Oh, I am 30, and everyone else is getting married, but why am I left out? Oh, I feel disappointed." When talking about marriage and love to those young men and women, their mouths might look like this... (making expressions, laughter) So, do you want love? "Yes." What kind of love? "God's love." Where is God's love? (Laughter) That is the problem.
Now, the question is how to find God's love, how to find a true person. That is the life of religion. We must understand that as human beings, we are dual beings with dual purposes. We have dual purposes. The subjective purpose and the objective purpose... the heart is the subject, and the body is the object. These must not fight.
Young men and women, when a man and a woman talk, before marriage, they must not become one. They must maintain distance. Then, by keeping that distance, they can play the game of becoming one.
So, what is a pure young man or woman? They are those who, while they like each other in their hearts, keep a distance from each other in appearance. That is the phenomenon. That is a pure young man or woman. Have you felt that here, young women? A man or woman who does not have that is not a pure young man or woman! Such a phenomenon occurs before maturity.
Then, when do they begin to act in which the body and heart can become one? It starts when love begins to sprout. That is how it is. You must emerge as a result of being able to bloom the flower of love with your heart and body becoming one through your maturity. The principle of creation is like that.
So, do you want to receive love, or do you want to give love? That is the question. Are you trying to receive, or are you trying to give? What is the principle? "To give." You must understand this. What comes first is not receiving but giving. Why is that? Because the creation of heaven and earth started from God, following God's love... God created to give love. What does He give? He gives the heart that represents heaven and the body that represents the earth, giving everything of body and heart. He gives everything.
Therefore, if we define the origin of the true history of love, we can establish true love in giving everything. Therefore, true love cannot be found where one does not try to give everything. This conclusion arises. It is not, "I will leave this handkerchief and give the rest." You must give everything. Here, you women will think the same. "What kind of husband should I get? Oh, I want a husband who gives everything, who gives more than his own life, body, and heart... a husband who gives everything." That is true. Do you want such a husband? "Yes." Then what will you do? "Oh, I like it. I want to receive everything, oh, that feels good." Will you just sit there and get bigger? (Laughter) Then that woman will also give more. If you give completely here, it will surely return as a plus from there. This is the principle of love. Then what happens to that love? It becomes yours, including that woman and her love. You can make that woman yours, and through that, you can find love. You can find both. Therefore, in loving, prosperity occurs. Prosperity occurs. Do you understand that? "Yes."
You know, these American men. These guys. Hippies...
When things are like this... You all thought that love was yours, saying, "Oh, my love." You thought it was yours. These thieves! Compared to this principle, how much... Is this human? It's worse than an animal. Now, will such people go to hell or heaven? "They will go to hell." Such people will go to the most extreme hell. If you have had such things in your past, repent! Now, do you understand?

Our task is to love God, humanity, and the earth. So now we must complete God's love here and bear fruit of God's love to offer it. When can we offer it? If we started with true love, will that love grow colder as time goes on, or will it grow stronger? "It grows stronger." That's the problem. In your 30s, it is deeper than in your 20s, in your 40s, it is more serious than in your 30s, and in your 50s, it is even more so. Ah! The older you get, the more you lean on a cane, the more you will love, right?

So, is it unhappy or happy for a person to grow old? "It is happy." Why? Why is that? Because the time comes when love bears fruit, the time when love becomes God's. You must understand that. It is precious because the fruit of love that God can take is being borne. What is God's love? Parental love, spousal love, and children's love; these three types of love are what the Unification Church has concluded. This is a great conclusion.

Now, I have prepared all of that. I became a true parent and truly loved my one child. I became a true spouse and truly loved. As a true son or daughter of God, I truly loved my siblings. I loved as a child. While loving those sons and daughters and the environment, what else must we love? We must love humanity and the earth. This is our task centered on love. Therefore, older people can train to love anyone, like their mother, their wife if she is older, like their grandmother, like their husband, and like their younger siblings. That is the ideal society.

Now, after finishing all of that, where do we go? While loving centered around this limited body, when we try to love the infinite absolute God, we cannot do it with a limited body. We must transcend the limit and freely act to love the infinite God, which leads to the conclusion that we must wear a body like God's.

For God, that moment is the moment of finally picking the fruit of love, but for me as a human, it is the moment of finally entering the realm where I can love the infinite God freely and one hundred percent. That moment is the moment of crossing the peak of death. As an existence that transcends time and space, I can freely act with God's thoughts and ideals, and as a counterpart of free love, I can live eternally. If that crossing is death, is that death unhappy or happy? "It is happy." Such logic... On the path to finding absolute true love, we can conclude that it is happy.

So, do you like dying? "Yes." You say dying is good. If you can find true love, then it's okay to die. This conclusion comes out. Do you understand? "Yes." If there is a way to do that, would you be willing to give up your life? Let me see a show of hands from those who can do that. You all have many desires, don't you? (Laughter)

We must move toward a higher and deeper path of love. Look at today; Teacher Moon is a global issue. When you say Reverend Moon, even in America... Now, why is it that Teacher Moon, despite enduring all kinds of humiliation and insults throughout his life, can endure and confidently expand from Korea to Japan and then to the world? It is because he knows this path, this path. In seeking a higher and deeper love, he knows that God is infinite and absolute, and that there is love that can dwell forever. Therefore, he seeks this path. The more the world opposes, the more he concludes that he can connect with God and receive love that the world cannot accept.

Now, let's say that a loving person has separated. Those who have separated are looking for each other, and among those who have searched for decades and those who give up after a year saying, "Oh, love and whatever, let's stop," which is more precious?

The more miserable it is, the more the glory of love shines. Is that right? "Yes." That's right. Therefore, if you have even one hour of leisure, you feel guilty in your conscience. You must work day and night without rest; then you can sleep well and digest your food. That is how your heart feels at ease. That is how you sleep well and enjoy your meals. Otherwise, your conscience and heart ache. Isn't that true for you all?

Why do you suffer selling peanuts and flowers in the Unification Church? Why do you suffer? You could pack your bags and run away whenever you want, but why don't you? It is because of your heart, your heart. This heart... Go and see. If you go, it is to the point of death. It is to the point of death. So after a few months, everyone comes back. (Laughter) So, is it good or bad to be infected with that disease? "It is good." Then there is nothing you can do. Do as your heart desires.

Your heart is the most tyrannical dictator in the world, a dictator. Do you know that? "Yes." Even if you feed all ten million people in New York, then it will say, "Hey! You, feed 220 million Americans." That is how the heart works. If you have fed all the people in New York, that should be enough, but then it says, "Now you must feed 220 million." 3)
The Centrality of Science and Absolute Value
Esteemed Chair, distinguished scientists, and respected professors and scholars! I am very pleased to express my warm welcome to all of you attending this International Conference on the Unification of Science, and I consider it a great honor to have you here.

As you already know, this conference was first held in the United States in November 1972, and has been held annually since then, with the second conference taking place in Tokyo the following November, the third in London, and now we are hosting the fourth conference here in the United States.

I would especially like to thank the professors who have continuously attended this conference each year. Your ongoing participation signifies that while you have thoroughly researched your respective fields, you have also dedicated your efforts to the common goal of the welfare of all humanity.

Today, in all fields, people tend to narrow their research scope to limited areas, thus losing sight of the overall purpose or the centrality of their tasks. As a result, they are losing the vitality that can only be generated and function through harmonious integration among their fields, drifting away from the fundamental motivation and purpose of science, which is to bring happiness to humanity. In extreme cases, people even find instances where their own inventions destroy their happiness.

The differentiation of science is similar to a body composed of scattered cells. When we examine the structure of the human body, we find that it consists of millions of cells interconnected in a network that allows the body to function with life. Humans have a central and subjective brain from which messages and commands pass through the spine and nerve endings to reach all cells, enabling millions of cells to function harmoniously. The eyes, as a subjective part of the body, have their own individual purpose while also contributing to the overall purpose of the body.

Every part of the human body has a dual purpose. Therefore, the pain of a single cell affects the entire body. Conversely, when each cell is healthy, the whole body is healthy. If the normal relationships or order among the cells are disrupted, humans will become ill. I believe that the ideal organization and structure of human society should resemble the structure of the human body.

Today's society, which has lost such relationships and order, is paralyzed and sick. Something has gone terribly wrong. Humanity, filled with chaotic and confused consciousness, has become frustrated. The explosive increase in population and the pollution and depletion of natural resources are not the only pressing issues. The illness of society lies within the essence of human existence.

To solve all these problems, humans must have a clean and sound mind to function effectively. What we need is not just an industrial or technological revolution, but a greater revolution of human consciousness. The resolution of social issues cannot be limited to natural sciences; it must transcend legal regulations and also impact the realms of social sciences, arts, and religion. The problems mentioned earlier are not confined to any one country. They are ultimate issues that affect humanity's history across past, present, and future generations.

Through this revolution of human consciousness, humans must be guided to use their research results in a highly creative and productive manner for the peaceful coexistence of all humanity. The ideal of humanity can only be realized when individual purposes and the overall purpose are perfectly harmonized.

Just as in all other research fields, in the field of natural sciences, immediate individual purposes must be achieved in conjunction with a broad overall purpose that will be realized over the long term for all humanity. Only in this way can we discover the true meaning of research results. To integrate all specialized research fields, we need a larger design and blueprint. Through this, we will realize our common ideals aimed at achieving integration.

The main purpose of this International Conference on the Unification of Science is to create such a blueprint. Therefore, I would like to propose a few thoughts related to this blueprint. Humans are aware that they possess life within themselves, originating from the highest dimension that is not limited by time and space. This source can be referred to as the universal mind or the first cause of all existence.

To give meaning to their lives, humans must understand the centrality of absolute value in the universe. By establishing a new world order where all humanity lives as brothers and sisters transcending nations and ethnicities, we can enjoy the ideal world of true peace and happiness.

To realize this, science must be examined from outside its own realm. Science policy must be determined while treating society as a whole. We must not lose sight of the central point of the overall purpose, which is that science is for the welfare of all humanity, not just for itself. In other words, to make the development of science meaningful in human daily life, humans must discuss and establish standards of value from a holistic perspective. Science begins with the study of visible external objects. However, science can also assist in understanding the internal aspects of the invisible realm or the spiritual dimension. Ultimately, these two realms must be integrated.

Therefore, we must be able to capture the central point located in the external world while simultaneously connecting it with the central point in the highest metaphysical world. Thus, when the former orbits around the latter as an unchanging axis, absolute meaning and value will be bestowed upon all existence in time and space.

In conclusion, I sincerely hope that all of you gathered here will freely present your valuable research results, exchange opinions openly, and discuss common issues that include the overall purpose of human welfare from a broad perspective. If you utilize the knowledge of your excellent fields of expertise in an integrated manner, I believe we can observe, comprehend, and resolve all existing problems in human society. In doing so, the centrality and absolute value of science in the realm of existence will be established and praised. I hope you will contribute to this vast task without reservation.

God's Plan Centered on America

Dear Congressman Ikod, members of Congress, and ladies and gentlemen! First of all, I sincerely thank you for the kind introduction by Congressman Ikod, and I appreciate your attendance despite your busy schedules.

Today, I consider it an honor to speak to you in this beautiful chamber of the U.S. Congress. This opportunity to address distinguished members of the U.S. Congress is my second chance. The first opportunity was on October 8, 1974. Today, about 14 months later, I stand here again.

During the past 14 months, I have increasingly become a subject of controversy in the American media. Various newspapers across the country have published extensive articles about me, and some magazines have featured my photo on the cover with cover stories. Some photos even made me look better than I actually am. I don’t know how to express my gratitude to the American media for making me so famous without paying a dime in advertising fees.
The focus of the American media is that I brainwash American youth. So, I would like to ask the wise American people one question. Are American people really so foolish as to be brainwashed by this Reverend Moon? No, they are not. That is not my answer either. I respect American people. 

On December 18, 1975 (Thursday), in the Caucus Room of the U.S. Capitol. 

However, I find it difficult to understand why the American people I respect would make such accusations, especially with violence. 

But today, I am not here to make excuses. I have come to testify the words that God has commanded me to convey. The rest will be judged by history. 

The title I want to speak about is "God's Plan Centered on America." 

The providence of God and the method to restore the ideal world of creation. 

To understand God's plan, we must first know what God's will is. God is eternal, unchanging, unique, and absolute. Therefore, God's will must also be eternal, unchanging, and absolute. When God created humanity, there was a purpose and an ideal, and if that purpose had been fulfilled, the world would have been a world united in love, where all humanity lives harmoniously as brothers and sisters under God as their parent, a world of one human family. 

In other words, that world would be a world unified in one purpose. This task of unification is the most important thing for humanity today, and that is why it remains exceedingly difficult. For individuals, it means the unification of body and mind, the unification of families, the unification of nations, the unification of East and West, and the unification of God and humanity. In other words, the world where God's purpose of creation is fulfilled is the world of unification. 

However, the reality today is far from this ideal world, so it is clear that something is fundamentally wrong. What could that be? It is because of the fall of our human ancestors, Adam and Eve, that God's will has not been realized. Therefore, individuals' bodies and minds are divided, families are divided, races are divided, nations are divided, East and West are divided, and God and humanity are all separated, living in division and disharmony. 

Such divided humanity is in a sick state, having lost its original function. God's purpose of salvation for humanity is to send a doctor who can diagnose and prescribe treatment for this sick humanity, to restore it to its original state before it became ill. This providence of salvation can be called the providence of restoration. The one who comes as the doctor is the Messiah. 

So, before sending the Messiah, what did God do, and what does the Messiah intend to do when He comes? That central religion is Judaism, and that central nation was the nation of Israel. The mission of that central religion and that central nation is to take the lead in fulfilling God's will, even if they face difficulties and bear the cross of sacrifice to save the entire world.

Thus, the providence of salvation, which is God's will and the will of the people, will be completed through the Messiah, and the unified ideal world will come. 

The mission of the central religion and nation shifted from Judaism and Israel to Christianity and America.

But do you have any regrets during this short period? You are dying. When I think about it, I wonder when it was… I don’t even know how old I am. How old am I? Am I 56 or 57? "You are 57." Am I turning 57 now? "Yes." Ah, you are better than me. It feels like a dream. It feels like a dream. When did this happen… I became like this because I was scolded, because I was scolded…

The Purpose of God's Creation of Humanity

So, from the 'principled perspective of the realistic mission,' when you return to your hometown, you must resolve this issue. You must repent and, in your short life, take care of your family, your children, and your church, and take responsibility for the way and this nation and the world. You must understand that this is the realistic mission. Do you understand? "Yes."

Look. When humans are born, think about the time when God created humans. God and the earth worked together. Right? When God created all things and said, "I will create a person," there must have been communication between God and all things, right? If there is no communication, what fun would there be? There must be communication. When God said to create a person, there must have been a covenant when God said, "You, all things, will input matter to create a person, and I will input my ability to create a person." 

What is that covenant? What is the good treaty between God and all things? Does God need money? Does He need diamonds? Does God need knowledge? Does He need power? What does He need? He needs nothing. What God needs is love. God cannot have love alone. Right? Do you understand? No matter how much of God He is, He cannot have love alone. It may exist, but it has not yet manifested in reality. Can love exist alone? No matter how absolute His power is, can He love while being alone? Can one love alone? "No."

That is why God also wants something. He has something He wants. What is that? It is love. He desires to have love. Then, when He asks, "What do you, all things, want?" what would you say? Of course, it would be to meet God. However, God is incorporeal. Therefore, you cannot interact freely with Him. You can only meet Him at special times. It is limited.

That is why, if there is a love that can be given and received without limitation, would you like that? "Oh, of course, I would." That is what matter says. It is the desire of all things. Therefore, all things also need a master or an object that can receive and give love every day.

That is why the logic that humans were created with a common purpose to have God's love and the love of all things is a valid logic. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Do you understand or not? "I understand." There is such a covenant in the universe. There is God's covenant.

Then why were humans born? They were born to love God and to love all things. This is the purpose and result of human birth. Do you understand? "Yes." Now you understand the purpose of human birth. Why were you born? "To love God." To love God, and then? "To love all things." To love all things. This is the purpose of human birth.

In other words, it can be said this way. Conversely, humans were born to receive God's love and to receive the love of all things. It is the same. If you love, you will be loved in return. Do you understand? It is the same whether you put it this way or that way.

Because of the existence of humans, God can have love, and because of the existence of humans, the love of the universe can be established, so it concludes that God could not help but create humans. This is where the purpose of God creating humans comes from. This is the purpose for which God created humans and needed them. That is why He created humans. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

You can only receive God's love after loving all things and humanity.

So have you loved all things? Have you loved God? Have you loved? From the perspective of the principle, when the subject establishes the object and gives and receives completely, they become one. When they become one, what emerges? An eternal center emerges. What is the eternal center? It is neither the subject nor the object, but what is it? It is love.

However, humans have become fallen beings and can no longer realize God's love and the love of the universe. Therefore, how can we find this again? We must do it according to the universal covenant. Do you understand? Then what is the universal covenant? The fact that humans have fallen means that they have lost their qualification as the masters of all things. Therefore, they must regain their qualification as the masters of all things.

To do that, what must be done? You must love all things. You must love the created beings. Do you understand? If a person on this earth can love all things instead of God, then according to that degree, they are bound to receive God's love naturally. This conclusion is clear. Do you understand? That is why you must love all things. A person who loves all things and loves humanity becomes qualified to receive God's love. A person who loves the world and the universe, who values and loves others more than their own life, can automatically receive God's love as something of that value. Do you understand? "Yes."

You cannot receive God's love directly. But you say, "I just need to receive God's love." However, that cannot be the case. If you had not fallen, you could receive God's love while loving all things, but because you have fallen, in the path of restoration, you must do the opposite. When you love all things, God's love arises according to the measure of that love. If the love of all things is considered negative love, then God's love is positive love, and as much as negative love arises, positive love will automatically arise. If two perfected people collide, there will be a spark. At that time, the whole world will be bright, and God will be happy, all things will be happy, and people will be happy. That is the day when the perfected Adam and Eve are blessed. Do you understand? "Yes."

Therefore, how can humans go to the kingdom of heaven? What is the absolute requirement for fallen humans? It is to love all things and to love humanity. How much should you love? You cannot return to the kingdom of heaven unless you love more than your own mother, your husband, or your children. Why? Because they are fallen people. A patriot in the fallen world, a loyal subject in the fallen world, cannot relate to that kingdom without being a greater patriot or loyal subject. The answer is clear. Do you understand? "I understand."

Everything must be organized. Only then will there be no confusion. Therefore, even when you step on the ground, you must think, "I have come here as a responsible person to uphold the universal covenant. While I am alive, I will walk the path of keeping the covenant." When dealing with people, you should think, "I will love for the sake of the universal covenant and to evoke the love of the kingdom of heaven. Whether people recognize it or not, I am a busy person on my path." You must think and strive day and night. The more you strive, the more God's love will come to you. Is that a principled statement or not? "It is." Isn't it true? "Yes."

That is why, throughout history, the greater the religion, the more it has emphasized love. It has emphasized God's love. How should we approach that love? We should not stop at love but transfer that love to love for all things and, furthermore, to love for humanity. It is in places that teach such love that religion begins. Do you understand? Religion does that, right? What does religion teach? Love! Buddhism speaks of compassion, and Christianity teaches to love people.

Therefore, how can you go to heaven and receive God's love? You cannot receive it directly. You must first love all things and love humanity before you can receive God's love. Why? Because you have fallen. Do you understand?

Let’s fulfill our realistic mission and become candidates for the world of love.

If humans had not fallen, as they grew older, the love between loving people would deepen, and that love would mature into complete love. It would enter the spherical love. If we received God's love during our youth, as we grow older, we can enter deeper into the world of God's love.

That is why death is ultimately the final gateway to reach the highest love. Therefore, the conclusion arises that death is not misfortune but happiness. Do you understand? "Yes." It means you can enter the most mature, complete love of God. Entering into that is entering into the core of the universe, the realm of ideals, so there, all my strength can encompass the entire world, and everything in the world can establish a subject-object relationship to unify with that ideal, making everything that belongs to it mine. That is why the world of love is the world of unity, and the concept that the world of love is my world is established. Thus, God, who has that love, is my God, and at the same time, that love of God becomes my love. That world is the ideal homeland of life.

Do you want to go to heaven? Do you want to receive God's love? Then love all things and love humanity. Otherwise, you cannot receive love. Love South Korea, love the world, love all people, and take responsibility to love people from the past, present, and future. This is the thought of the Unification Church. It is not just about the present people. It is about taking responsibility to love people from the past, present, and future. That is God's wish. So, with God's wish, what can I not do? I must strive until I die. The more I grow, the more God's love will come… right? When a complete negative arises, a complete positive arises. When a complete positive arises, I hope for that, and if I create a complete negative according to that principle, we will gradually become one.

In this way, I will explode centered around myself. The completion of love cannot be achieved only by God. It is through me that all love is completed. This astonishingly valuable existence is 'me.' Without this 'me,' God cannot move. How wonderful is that? Do you understand? "Yes." It is all the same. Therefore, let us fulfill all our realistic responsibilities and missions and go to that world, and become candidates in that world. We are not frauds. We aim to become candidates.

Now, knowing that, in 1976, be meaningful individuals, as I leave with this purpose to engage in a great struggle in the world, I feel sorry for Korea when I leave. If you love this country on behalf of me, Kim Il-sung will never invade. Do you understand? "Yes." Kim Il-sung will not invade. If he does, the communists will perish. That is how I see it. If he invades, he will not be allowed to do so. The leaders above are not fulfilling their responsibilities, those sons of bitches. They all need to repent.

So you must take on that role. Since we are at the forefront of this country, even if we get shot, we will take the first hit, and even if we get beaten, we will take the first hit… Why? Because God has the way of salvation and the love of the path. I stand at the forefront to save this country, to bring in even one more person, so I will take the hit and leave this country behind. Would God dislike that? Would God punish me? Ultimately, He cannot punish because of those people. Do you understand? "Yes."

Therefore, until May of next year, you must sincerely… Asia is in crisis now. I am thinking that new hope will emerge from one place. I am seeing that dreamlike reality unfolding. In 1976, that reality must unfold to match the time of providence… That is how I think. Do you understand? "Yes."

With a solemn determination, give your best at this once-in-a-lifetime moment.

Do you have any questions for me? You didn’t have lunch, did you? "I ate." Remember well what I said today… Now, what time is it tomorrow evening? "It’s at 8:30." If it’s 8:30, we must leave. So there will be a national meeting at 9:00 on the 31st. Everyone will gather for the meeting. It is to welcome the New Year… So before 9:00 on the 31st, you must return.
It must be done. What time can we arrive at six minutes past six in the morning? "It will be at five twenty-two."
Next time you come, you must bring good news, but I am worried right now. We are in a position where we must deploy 10,000 people. Only then will we surpass 200,000. If this time you can just blow the wind well and it goes according to your plan, it will feel like launching a satellite. That's exactly how it will feel. Just like when Apollo 11 went to the moon, the world was paying attention; this is such an event. The Reverend Moon's plan is like the Apollo launch plan; that is the game we are in. It is a game that has never existed in history.

Knowing this, when you return, don’t just let your eyes be bloodshot, your feet sore, your nose runny, and your blood drained... Don’t do that. We must be able to say, "Let’s fill it up tightly until the teacher returns, restore this country massively, and become those who can praise the teacher's victory on a grand scale." It must be like this. When the time comes, you will only need to put in your effort, and it will be more than enough. The time will come. It will change. It will happen like this.

With this, by the end of the 1976 Washington Conference, the spiritual world will tilt from 90 degrees to 45 degrees. So, when a great wave occurs in the three Asian countries, an organization capable of pushing out the communists will be formed. If such an event occurs by the middle of 1977, the world will not be far from being able to be shaped according to the teacher's thoughts.

If that does not go well, we will move into the 1980s, and if things do not go as the teacher wishes until the 1980s, it will be extended by 20 years into the 2000s. If that happens, the teacher will be 80 years old. Do you understand? At 81... Just like Moses was 81 when he was going on the second journey of the Canaan gospel, it will surely be like that. When the third seven-year course ends at 60, isn’t 20 years 80 years? That will be in the 2000s.

So, it’s not far off. Whether we extend it by 20 years or not depends on you. If it is extended, how great will the damage be to the spiritual world? The spirits in the spiritual world will have to wait for hundreds of millions of years. For them, a day of waiting is like a thousand years. So how astonishing would that be? I know that. Standing at this truly once-in-a-lifetime moment, if we seize it, the universe will come rushing in; if we miss it, the universe could drift away. This is a solemn time. Do you understand? This is in accordance with principle.

So, knowing this, as the teacher goes to America, you must fulfill your relative responsibilities so that you can establish the prestige of being the subject nation on behalf of the teacher. Do you understand? "Yes." Will you do it or not? "I will." So, will you fill the newly built church by the time I return, or not? "I will fill it."

For this conference, everyone has sworn to evangelize a certain number of people and is going out at dawn to work. They promised to deploy 5,000 from the West and 5,000 from New York, but if 5,000 and 5,000 do not match, the New York conference will fail.

So, by the time the teacher returns, we must lay that foundation in Korea. We cannot leave the church empty. Let’s see a show of hands for those who have built a church! Who has a church? Oh, quite a few. Now, let’s see a show of hands for those who do not have one. "Oh, it’s not an A type..." No, it’s not just A type; there are those without a church right now. "There are no places without a church. There are houses, though." Other than A type or newly built two-story houses, or places like Buan, are there any other churches? "No." "There are none." That’s not many. It’s not many at all.

I’m in pain in my legs... Give me a chair. "Will the meeting be held here for a bit tomorrow?" Hold on. I will give a few instructions, and then I will finish the meeting... I have busy things to do tomorrow. My back hurts, my butt hurts, in fact, there’s no place that doesn’t hurt. I will go at eight-thirty tomorrow evening, so should we gather around four? Should we gather around three? Everyone should gather in Cheongpadong. I will talk a bit and then leave. "Only the leaders?" No, those near Seoul. "There are about 1,300 members in Seoul..." Even if a thousand attend, we can set conditions for attendance.

Shall we do it at three or three-thirty? "Yes." "Will the regional leaders also attend?" The regional leaders will attend, right? If they don’t want to, then forget it. (Laughter) "It’s not that they don’t want to, but the place is so crowded that they are standing outside the door..." What’s wrong with standing? Isn’t it good? Should we do it here? "If we do it here, when Father goes out..." It’s good when I go out. So let’s do it here. (Murmuring) If they stand, will they all come in? "Even sitting, over a thousand can come in." Then that’s fine. Still, it would be better to do it at the headquarters. That’s how it should be. Those who really want to come can come, and those who don’t, it’s okay if they don’t come. "Where will the location be?" Let’s do it at Cheongpadong Church. "If we say to come to Cheongpadong, will only the church leaders come? The general members will stay away." "The headquarters church is too small, so it’s impossible." What’s impossible? The floor is small, so we have to build the headquarters church. If all the local churches are built, we should build the headquarters church, right? This time, you all must help build the headquarters church. Do you understand what I mean? "..." How many churches are there in total? Even if each church contributes ten thousand won, that would be fine. (Murmuring) I left the records I had and didn’t bring them.

Now, I will stop, and tomorrow I will just give a few instructions. The teacher will stop, and Bohee, shall we report a bit? "Yes." Have you had dinner? You haven’t had dinner, right? "Yes." Let’s have dinner. Then let’s pray and eat.

<Prayer> Beloved Father! We deeply long for the day when we can block the flow of history and settle all your sorrows and debts. We earnestly hope and wish that all your desires to transform the sad days into victorious days will be realized through our dedication.

Father! The year 1975 is coming to an end. As we greet the new year of 1976, we are entering a critical time when we must issue a final command through the guardians to strike a decisive blow in the historical and providential battles, and we realize it is a fearful time.

Father! Now, we have a mission to cross over to America and must engage in fierce battles. We know that we cannot lose the land that you desire to pass on to your children and your world. We earnestly ask that this entire Yankee Stadium conference be concluded in a way that you orchestrate, in a way that pleases you.

Along with that, this homeland where the teacher was born, this nation must fulfill its prestige and face as a nation of faith, so your children scattered across the nation have gathered here.

Father! We have come to realize the immense responsibility of the realistic mission from a principled perspective. We now recognize our lack of loyalty and our lack of filial piety, and we have come to understand what the original path of humanity that you desire is.

As a governor, as a parent, as a church leader, we must fulfill our responsibilities and equip ourselves with the authority of sons who can triumph over Satan, praising the glory of victory before you, returning to embrace the loving Father, shedding the tears of a thousand years of sorrow, and hoping for the world of your comfort and love to begin. This is our wish as your children. Father, please have mercy and guide us.

Now, Father, please protect this land that remains and safeguard the thirty million. Moreover, please be with the people in North Korea. We have the responsibility to repel the groups of villains who are ruling through illegal conquest, so we pledge to unite and gather the people of South Korea as a volunteer army desired by Heaven to advance north and subdue them, allowing for unification and more.

We thank you for granting us this time. Now, for those who will remain and return, may they hold the shield of victory in the upcoming battlefield, Father, please be with them, and may it be days where they can pledge to advance.

If the church that has been built is empty, Father, the face of this child, your face, the face of the Unification Church, and the face of this nation will be damaged, so please allow it to be filled and more than enough. May these people offer everything with gratitude, and may Heaven have no choice but to cooperate, and those with a heart cannot help but be drawn in unknowingly. We earnestly hope that such movements of Heaven will sweep across this peninsula.

And so, on the day we meet again, may we be a group that looks forward to the results of victory while enduring and fighting. 

The teacher will now bear the heavy burden of the fierce battle in America alone, but when we realize that you are protecting and walking with him, we will run breathlessly toward the day that pleases Heaven, and we want to hasten that step with gratitude. We earnestly hope that everything will be accomplished appropriately before you on this path.

Father, who knows how to protect this world, we earnestly wish for you to protect it. We ask that you bless the sons who will take on heavy responsibilities and move in Japan, and may you establish a foothold to defend Asia before the will of Heaven and a pillar that can lay a bridge for world peace.

May you be with us in all things, and please protect the children in Bellevedere, Barrytown, and East Garden until we meet again, and may we meet in joy.

We earnestly request that your protection and peace be granted to all your children, and we pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.
